Words for the Birthday Celebration of Kwon Jin
<Prayer (I)> Today, on the 21st day of the first month of the lunar calendar in 1976, which corresponds to February 20th in the solar calendar, is the day when Kwon Jin was born on this earth and is celebrating his first birthday. Father, please bless him.
Kwon Jin, who was born as the fifth son in our family under your blessing, may you be present with us as Heaven and Earth watch over us. Moreover, as this occasion represents your banquet, which you have prepared, please graciously accept it. I sincerely hope that all spirits in the spirit world, all people on earth, and countless descendants who will come to this earth will celebrate this day of the baby as a pride before your will.
Although there have been many babies, this celebration represents all their hopes, and with the authority of your nation, we celebrate this first birthday. Celebrating the birth of Kwon Jin on the historical foundation that has opened the way for the spirit world and the physical world to welcome the True Parents is to establish a special condition for all spirits to welcome the babies.
Furthermore, with all the brothers from the East Garden—Ye Jin, Hyo Jin, In Jin, Heung Jin, Eun Jin, Hyun Jin, Guk Jin, and Kwon Jin—gathered here, representing America and visiting Korea, may you bless us. Connecting Asian and Western civilizations.
February 20, 1976 (Friday), at the Headquarters Church (Cheongpa-dong 1-ga).
* The title of this message was added by the editor.
8   Words for the Birthday Celebration of Kwon Jin
May this banquet be a day of joy that you will personally enjoy, Father.
Father! While commemorating the birth of this baby, may it also be allowed to be remembered as a new day in this universe. I sincerely hope that your foundation of blessing will spread from this land of Korea to the whole world.
Father! I earnestly ask that you accept this banquet with complete joy. As a parent performing your banquet, I sincerely ask that this procedure, conducted in your name, be a joy within your will, and I pray all these words in the name of the True Parents. Amen.
<Prayer (II)> Beloved Father, today is the 21st day of the first month of the lunar calendar in 1976, which corresponds to February 20th in the solar calendar, and it is the day when Kwon Jin is celebrating his first birthday. Father, I thank you for blessing this day. I am grateful for allowing us to celebrate this day again under your love and protection for a year.
May this banquet be a blessing where countless babies in the heavenly kingdom and many children on earth can receive blessings together through the growth of this baby.
Please allow this time of celebration centered on your name. Moreover, as we celebrate this banquet together with the brothers in the East Garden, Father, please accept it. May this be a new origin from which we can praise your eternal victory in front of all people and all worlds.
Today, because of this baby… May all beings celebrate the day of the True Parents' birth on the foundation of conditions in the spirit world and the physical world, and may they be blessed on the day of the birth of the True Children. I know that this banquet, which is allowed to be celebrated for the first time on this Korean land, has historical significance, and I sincerely hope that all beings can rejoice in the blessing of new life and praise this glory for eternity, and may you bless us to head directly to the kingdom of victory.
I earnestly ask that celebrating the birth of this baby is not just for this baby alone but establishes a day to celebrate the joyful birth of Heaven and Earth. I sincerely hope that this holy banquet becomes a pride for you, a pride for all spirits in the spirit world, a pride for all parents on earth, and a pride for all babies. I earnestly ask that you accept everything with joy, and I pray all these words in the name of the True Parents. Amen.
(After reciting my pledge five times, Yoo Kwang-ryeol, the head of the Cultural Department of the Association (currently the chairperson of the Historical Compilation Committee), recited a congratulatory poem titled "Take That First Step.")
<Words> Thank you for gathering here today to commemorate our Kwon Jin's first birthday. And why is this day being celebrated so specially? Our Kwon Jin was born in America and has American citizenship. At the same time, he is Korean. What does this signify? It holds significant meaning in establishing a condition for Western civilization to connect with Asian civilization.
As you know, previously, when celebrating the birthday of the True Parents, no spirits in the spirit world had the opportunity to celebrate the day of the True Parents' birth, but now you are commemorating this day. Many spirits in the spirit world cannot stand in a position to celebrate the day of the True Parents' birth, and they have not been able to celebrate the day of the birth of the True Children, so I believe that the opportunity for the spirit world to celebrate the day of the True Parents and True Children is determined by this time.
Therefore, the spirit world is now establishing an order and moving toward one world. Because you have conducted the Unification Ceremony, the spirit world stands in a position corresponding to the angelic world, serving the True Parents in the Adam family, centered on the True Parents' children, and entering an era where such origins are determined.
That is why the spirit world will enter the world of the archangels, and on the ground, it will enter the Adam world that needs to be recreated. Then, who will carry out the recreation? It must be the Adam who stands in the position of God and you, who stand in the position of the perfected Adam. Therefore, our mission is the restoration of Adam. It is to resurrect those Adams who could not be perfected and move them to the position of perfection. This is the revival history of the Unification Church that must develop into the world in the future.
In that sense, today, the day of Kwon Jin's birth is significant historically because it is celebrated in Korea, representing all the babies, and I know that there has been guidance in the spirit world to prepare well for this occasion.
In that sense, I hope that you will attend this celebration, representing your family members, and think of it as a day of representation for celebrating future generations of children.
<Prayer> All beings of heaven and earth are created through your creative artistry, and Adam and Eve, who were created as your sons and daughters to govern all beings, were meant to govern all things. I know that since that day when our human ancestors left a history of resentment, they have gone through a long history of sorrow without seeing the day of fulfilling their wishes.
I am grateful that today, through the Unification Church and the names of the True Parents and True Children born in Korea, a historical new comprehensive settlement has been prepared, allowing us to meet the day you wished for.
To go through this process… Centered on the Israelite people, Christianity, and the Unification Church today, we celebrate the day of the birth of our Kwon Jin baby, which determines the family origin that connects Western civilization and Asian civilization, and I hope that you bless this time, Father.
May countless spirits in the spirit world, countless descendants on earth, and many children who have come and gone on this earth, as well as many children who will come to this earth, be able to head directly to the heavenly kingdom centered on heaven, and I sincerely thank you for allowing this first birthday celebration of Kwon Jin to take place in this historical land of Korea. Centered on all families in the spirit world, may the history of opening the way to the heavenly kingdom be achieved through this baby's first birthday.
Moreover, I believe that those brothers and sisters in the East Garden who could not attend are also present in spirit, and I hope you bless this time. I know that the fact that this celebration is taking place centered around this baby, where the West and Asia unite to celebrate together, is a focal point of historical origin, so please bless this occasion.
Thus, from this time forward, many children born on this earth will receive your blessings and will be born as victorious sons and daughters who are not under the dominion of this evil world. I earnestly ask that this time, starting from Kwon Jin and all blessed family babies, as well as all sons and daughters born in many families on this earth, receive your blessings.
I earnestly request that all beings created in your name, starting from the True Parents' name, become one with the names of true children, and unite with true tribes, nations, and the world to fulfill the ideal world of your original goodness and receive glory.
I thank you for allowing this time to be an important global opportunity to open the way, and I sincerely hope that infinite mercy, victory, and authority will fill the entire universe, and may only the path of absolute obedience to the direction you guide be revealed.
I know that the day is not far off when any group opposing your will will submit before your will, so I earnestly ask that you bless us even more to head directly to the kingdom of victory, following the authority of the whole, and I pray all these words in the name of the True Parents. Amen.

Ability and Achievements
Were there not special forces members in the past? If so, please raise your hands. Were all of you district leaders? "Yes, district leaders, special forces." How many people? "Twelve." Is that all? "Yes." Is there anyone else? "There are others." Who else? "Is there anyone who is not here among the district leaders?" "We decided on twelve at that time."
Please write down those names.
The Education System of Barrytown
Also, please raise your hands if you have been in a public position in the church for over ten years. Over fifteen years, please raise your hands. Now, please stand up one by one. Please write down how many people you have evangelized over the past fifteen years. (Laughter) How many people has the most successful person evangelized? "Among those who remain?" Then it would be among those who remain. You know, those who can become members. You understand, right? You will calculate that as you evangelize… Now, the American members, foreign members will be left behind. In America, they are evangelizing three people a month… In the future, Korea and Japan will all be the same.
The teacher has created Barrytown in America and is currently educating there.
February 6, 1976 (Friday), at the Headquarters Church.
* This message was given during a national district leaders' meeting, and according to the order, it should have been included in volume 83, but for editing reasons, it was included in volume 84.
14   Ability and Achievements
We have trained 300 people in the 120-day training until last December, and they have been assigned nationwide. The goal for those assigned is to evangelize three people a month, and they are currently working towards that.
So Korea will also be made to do the same in the future, so please listen carefully. Those who have been educated cannot do as they please. Based on a nationwide activity system, we will focus on the best methods… Centered on who is representative nationwide in evangelism… That must be fully controlled by our Barrytown educational institution, here at the training center.
And until now, there have been district leaders, but those district leaders will be subordinate to the Barrytown educational institution. Also, district leaders must be from the training center instructors. That is how the system has been created. Therefore, the activity members who are going out across the nation, namely the pioneering members, are the teachers who directly guide them. That is why the educated teachers will directly guide them and also be present on-site… (The recording cuts off briefly)
Even looking at Korea, if you graduate from a university, they just give you a diploma and send you out. However, what you learned at that university does not yield results in the current society. It becomes completely disconnected and must be separated from each other. Therefore, while there are institutions in universities, the relationship with their graduates and alumni is ambiguous. If the university institution had a stronger organization to manage its alumni and went around locally to see how they could utilize their expertise after graduation, they could gather data and select some people to be recognized by the state. If such an education system is created, it could significantly contribute to society.
However, simply providing education and stopping there means that what has been learned does not yield results in current society. There is a flaw in that. Therefore, in the future, what kind of system should we create within our will? We must manage everything from where we have educated. And we will create a district system where the district leaders will directly go to the local area and bring excellent people from among the locals to become future leaders and instructors. Therefore, they will have a clear understanding of all activities related to the local area. Thus, those who are currently pioneering will have the ability to guide. They will coach everyone.
So, we plan to create a system of first-class, second-class, and third-class district leaders. Once this is established, the skills learned through education can be fully demonstrated in the local area. Therefore, we will experiment with that while providing education.
of organizations. The association organization, the victory alliance organization, and the economic organization are completely separate. Therefore, the economic leaders of each state must hold meetings similar to the current church leaders' meetings to create a nationwide system for making money, and the same goes for the victory alliance.

In this way, we can create a system that allows for the development of leaders who can guide the nation. The goal is to train individuals who can lead at a national level, ensuring that they are well-equipped with the necessary skills and knowledge. 

This approach is not just about individual evangelism; it's about creating a structured system that can effectively mobilize resources and people for a common purpose. By focusing on training and development, we can ensure that our members are not only committed but also capable of achieving significant results.

In conclusion, the methods we have discussed are designed to create a robust framework for evangelism and community engagement. By implementing these strategies, we can ensure that we are not only growing in numbers but also in the quality of our outreach efforts. This is essential for the long-term success of our mission.
is how it is done. By taking a separate route like this, they can freely choose the path they want to take in the future.

Generally, what is the current trend? People engaged in economic activities all say, "I also want to be educated and do some evangelism... but just doing economic activities won't work..." This creates a psychological loss. While doing something, they always have the mindset of "I need to do this quickly..." which means their genuine effort doesn't come out.

If everyone is sent out to pioneering areas, those who fall behind will inevitably follow their own destiny... No one can avoid going in the direction of the economy for their entire life. We have experimented with this. So, when they psychologically think, "I absolutely cannot evangelize. This is all there is!" they end up just working hard. Whether they are doing something trivial or not, they cannot avoid putting in their full effort. This shows the significant impact of psychological influence.

Starting from what they are least good at... If that happens, since they are falling short... then they can either go into the economic field or the victory field. After that, there is the international task force, so they are told to go to the international task force. Under this kind of training... Since direct guidance is provided at this training center, it is quite effective.

While evangelizing, if they encounter "there is this problem, what should I do?" and immediately call Barrytown, the support staff will always answer the phone and give instructions. "Do it like this and this." They will coach them through everything. Do you understand? Therefore, even if they lack professional insight, they can receive coaching and carry it out as it is, leading to rapid development. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes."

Korea should follow the American system
Korea will also become like that in the not-so-distant future. So what should be done? Until now, when you all engage in trade, you have done everything your own way. From now on, in the era of systems... To move the nation and the world, you cannot operate with your own arbitrary methods. The organizational system must move. To move the entire Republic of Korea, even if there are tens of millions of you, you cannot do it separately.

It is necessary to have an organizational system centered around a structured training system, and as that organizational system becomes completely refined into one, it will inevitably develop both vertically and horizontally. This is how it is viewed. Without this training, we cannot move the world in the future. Do you understand? "Education should be done like this, and the activities of the Unification Church should be done like this." As soon as anyone comes in, they should be made aware of this, and everyone will understand it. They will all recognize it, and once they start eating, they will just run around like that.

Therefore, on the day you evangelize, you must definitely provide training. Even if the trade center does it, a 21-day training should be conducted. When evangelizing, that person is not just their own person. They are offering people to the nation. If the system for pioneering is fully established, it is acceptable to send the evangelized people back to the field centered around them. If they receive guidance from the evangelized person, it can yield even more effective results, so that method can be adopted. However, if that is not possible, then it is necessary to lead nationwide and adopt effective methods. 

The method and results
When viewed from the perspective of the entire Unification Church, centered around the nationwide Unification Church, this is seen as a benefit. Shouldn't it be done that way? You need to know that such work is being done and that you are being trained in that way.

Then, what would happen if you placed the trade centers in Korea in such a world? They would truly become like country folks, rural people. They would be bewildered and become like country people. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes."

In the same way, you all should, just like what is done at the Barrytown training center, if you have completed a 21-day training, you should arrange those people to be able to conduct a 3-day training or a 1-week training, and do so in all directions, engaging in 24-hour activities. It doesn't have to be that everyone is doing it alone. Create A, B, C, D, and establish east, west, north, and south, and conduct lectures. If there is even one person listening to the lecture, go to that house. Go to that house and say, "I will conduct a lecture at your house, so please let me use your room!" and when that is done, the district leaders will go around and give lectures.

You should conduct a 3-day training! So, you conduct the training. And you should conduct a 1-week training! If you do this, after experiencing the 3-day training and the 1-week training, everyone will know, and then if you gather them and conduct a 3-week training, they will become core members. If you keep spreading that, what will happen? If it keeps spreading like that, the more you do it, the more it multiplies. If there are ten people, they will be doing it in ten places, and if there are a hundred people, they will be doing it in a hundred places, so if all of them are not idle and become responsible for the 3-day training and the 1-week training, then the number of people under their command will automatically expand.

Don't think that you have to do everything yourself. Like the branches of a tree, "Oh! I came from one branch, so I will stay only on this branch." But do branches grow leaves here? Just like a tree, you should be centered and extend in all directions... Therefore, when the district leader conducts the 21-day training, they can say to someone who has completed the 21-day training, "You are responsible for the 1-week training," and to someone who has completed the 1-week training, "You should try conducting the 3-day training!" This can be done in any number of ways.

A person who knew nothing about the Unification Church just a week ago, after receiving a week of training, if they decide to conduct a 3-day training lecture, how enthusiastic will they be? By strengthening the organizational structure into an educational system, the more the number increases nationwide, the more proportional the increase will be... This is scientific. Do you understand? This is the system we are currently strengthening, this kind of system.

Therefore, those who cannot give lectures cannot be members of the Unification Church. If they have already received a week of training, they must be qualified to conduct a 3-day training. This is how it should be thought. If they have received a 3-week training, they become qualified to conduct a 1-week training. Because of this, they must give lectures. Therefore, as soon as they come in, they should grab the principle book, study it, summarize the key points, and after a week, gradually expand from there, and skills will naturally develop.

Now the era of group leaders' evangelism
Now, such activities are being conducted in Western society. In Japan, similar activities have been directed recently. Looking at it now, there are a dozen or so people who have been in the church for 15 years, thirty-some people... This is not acceptable. Can they say they have contributed after joining the Unification Church? Can they ask for a salary from the headquarters? What kind of people are those who have evangelized?

If they are like governors who can move a country, that would be one thing, but if they are all what you might call the lower ranks, what can they do by evangelizing? They should evangelize people who can lead the masses, not those who are dragged along by the masses... Whether they exist or not... It becomes a problem instead. Those who want to rely on others, what good does it do to evangelize them?

You all have entered the international era now. Do you understand? "Yes." Korea will also be like that in the future. Let's create such an organizational structure! Every six months, there should be a personnel reshuffle. So, new capable people will be recognized in the future. If you look at it, you will immediately know. They should be removed, and personnel adjustments should be made accordingly. Therefore, the Unification Church must recognize that it has already passed the national level era. Do you understand? "Yes."

As a civilized nation in the West, the members from the United States and Europe are conducting practical education under such a system, and not only education but also engaging in practical activities with effectiveness to challenge the world. You must understand that they are challenging the home country, Korea.

We cannot have the same attitude as in the past. If you go to the host country and ask how many people you have evangelized after 15 years of activity, it would be 20 people... Is that possible? No, it is not. We have passed the era of individual evangelism, and you are all in the era of evangelizing group leaders, group leaders. Now, they are all big-headed individuals. You cannot just leave it to the heads of organizations. You must know how to utilize them.

And from now on, you all must engage in cultural activities. Things like movie films... Hey, association president! "Yes." You must create movie films and strengthen cultural activities nationwide, across the country. In the future, every trade center must have at least one projector, and even if they cannot, they should have dozens of films ready. Just having that will allow you to show good movies to neighbors, even dozens of miles away. If there are 50 films in Jeollanam-do, if you rotate them weekly, it will take a year. Do you understand? You can show new movies every day. Isn't that right? If you show just ten films like this, you can do whatever you want. This is the kind of thinking we should have.

Now, the Ministry of Culture is also making various films to engage in cultural activities nationwide, to promote. There are many good films. Can't you borrow them as much as you want? There are public relations offices in every county and district, right? "Yes." Therefore, if there are just 50 films in one province, since there are 52 weeks in a year, if you have just 52 films, you can continuously show new movies every week for a year to enlighten people. In rural areas, if you say, "Come to watch a movie," people will come from 20, 30, or even 50 miles away. Once they get a taste for it, they will keep coming back if you say, "We do this every week." 

What is this all about? If you do this for about six months, everyone will follow what you want. Why wouldn't they? Do you think it is possible or not? "It is possible."

Next, if we prepare microbuses, we can gradually bring in heads of organizations and anyone else. Then, we can also make a profit. If hundreds of people gather every week, what can we do? We can sell food. That is how business works. The issue of a few thousand won in salary is not the problem. It is about making tens of thousands of won in profit in a single day.

Isn't that right? Since the bosses are here, they will sit and watch, feeling good, and they will want to eat something sweet, peanuts, or drink something... That is human nature. When they are watching, the atmosphere is such that they cannot help but spend money. Everyone has a bit of money. If they come and completely let go of what they brought, this is a kind of business that has no equal. It can yield more effectiveness than charging people to watch. This is the kind of thinking we should have. If we prepare thousands of chicken legs and say, "You eat! You eat!" everyone will take one. How great is that? If you just think like this, there will be plenty of economic resources.

If a good movie is shown in a rural area, a significant number of people will gather. Not just hundreds, but thousands will come. Isn't that right? That is how it is. If you set it up like this, what will you sell? There are many children. If you organize a Sunday school with all the local kids, you will be able to reach everyone within 20 miles. You need to use your head, your brain.

Now, there aren't many people opposing the Unification Church, right? What do you think? The established churches are just collapsing and struggling, and those who are crawling along are saying, "Oh! What about the Unification Church?" That kind of thing doesn't work. Therefore, when opposition arises, we should dance and sing along with it. If we create that joyful atmosphere and move east, they will follow us, and if we move west, they will follow us too. If we do this for just a few days, everyone will become friends. If everyone agrees that it is good, then they will all be organized and can do anything.

Utilize the new village leaders trained at the central training center
Also, at our International Victory Federation Central Training Center, we have trained 50,000 new village leaders nationwide. Ah, you guys don't have the capacity to digest that... Why can't you digest it? Can you or can't you? Do you know that those new village leaders have come to the central training center for education? Do you know or not? "I know." Do you really know? "I know." Raise your hand if you don't know. Those who don't know won't raise their hands. Those guys should be struck by lightning! (Laughter) That shows their indifference.

Sitting on this multi-dimensional foundation, if you pull a line here and pull a line there, you will get caught. Everyone who has been educated at this training center is amazed by the Unification Church. When they come... If they are going to meet the village chief, they should at least wear a suit, even if they have to borrow one, and go looking sharp, putting on some oil, and matching their tie color well. They should not let the village chief think, "That guy came to us because he is in debt." If they look shabby when the Unification Church is being looked up to, that is the end. That cannot happen. So, they should dress neatly when they go.

Then, when they go, they should confidently say, "I am the church leader here, and you came back from training this time. Thank you very much. Now, we are comrades in fighting against communism and unifying the village." They should ask how old they are and say, "I am this age, so you can be my older brother, and I will be your younger brother." If they can bond as good brothers, they will visit each other, sleep over, and eat together. (Laughter) Why are you laughing? Are you laughing because you like it or because you are disgusted? "Because I like it." You like it? Why can't we do such good things? (Laughter)

That is how it is. Everything in the world is like that. Without such a mindset, how can you lay a foundation in someone else's neighborhood, where there is territorialism? There is territorialism, right? "Yes." With such a mindset, do you think it will work? If you don't have that mindset, then pack up everything. Even if you get cursed at, if you look this way and get cursed, look that way and smile... "Oh, is that the level of cursing? If there is something like this, I would like to hear it." So, let them tell you. "I have only heard that! I haven't heard this! There is also this." After that, when they come to the Unification Church, you teach them to oppose it once. If you do it like that, their faces will completely change. Even if you tell them to do that, they cannot. "No matter what that person says, they will digest it all, and since I am already like a grandfather to them, their opposition won't work." That is how it is.
While asking that, receiving the frequency smoothly, and smiling gently, saying, "Oh, is that all you know?" and then quickly adding, "Not just that, our teacher knows much more…." If you do that while smiling gently…. That’s humor, you see, humor. If you do it this way, you can push everything away within three minutes, but this is like being a slowpoke. If you do it just once like that, everything will break apart. Why is that? If you oppose it, you need to play a game where you pull back and forth with humor in a fun way. You need to have that kind of courage. Depending on the situation, when you see that person, you can tell everything by their personality. Once you look, you know right away. There are nervous types, medium types, and calm types. If you determine that guy is a "nervous type," then no matter what, if you make them talk, they will spill everything in no time. After that, you meet them for a day, then for two days…. Don’t think it’s strange.

And then, "Oh, by the way, you seem to have quite a bit of interest in the Unification Church." No matter how you think about it, that’s the case. (Laughs) In the end, it means you know that much, so how can you not be interested? "Then a little more. I’ll teach you a bit more." After saying that, "What you know is…." You can always push back against those who oppose you and have a conversation. By doing this, even if you are higher up, if you become bigger than that person, you sit on top. Isn’t that right? That’s how you should think. What good is it to get heated for no reason? You just end up feeling bad. If you approach it with that mindset, even if you feel bad, it can be fun. That’s how you should think.

All the Saemaul leaders across the country, all the village heads and leaders, have received education, so why can’t they digest this? Raise your hands if you’ve ever visited. Look at these kids! These kids! They need to be beaten until their bones break, until they are battered to pieces. In the era of restoration providence, a day feels like a thousand years, and in this current era, the church leaders responsible for their missions have such materials that even the king's stick can fall apart. Yet they don’t even go to find it, can’t digest it.

Write a journal and engage in activities.
No matter how many years you go on like this, you’ll only get that far. You’re just producing little loaches. You can’t have high hopes relying on you. You need to throw all this away and educate anew to create a new system. That’s the only conclusion that can be drawn. Now, do you have any objections? If you continue like this…. In the future, foreigners will come and say, "In about 20 years, that’s an incompetent Korean," and you’ll be in trouble. Do you understand what I’m saying? "Yes." Get your act together.

President of the association! "Yes." From now on, we need to educate in that regard. Now, the president himself must do this too. Every month, he should evangelize at least one person…. Even in Japan, they put up posters everywhere and pray daily, thinking, "Today, I’ll put in one more hour than yesterday, and I’ll make a little more effort, and I’ll say one more word." This kind of mindset needs to be cultivated so that even if they can’t do it, they can at least meet the standard of reaching one person; if they do the same as yesterday, they won’t get anywhere for a thousand years.

God's Cooperation and Our Responsibility
<Prayer> Beloved Father, this morning we bow down before Your presence with all our hearts and bodies, so please find us with a heart of love, mercy, and compassion. <Words> We, the members of the Unification Church, are well aware that this purpose is being advanced under God's cooperation. God's will cannot be fulfilled by human beings alone. Everything is achieved through God's cooperation and human responsibility.
So here, God's cooperation and our responsibility… For that, God must cooperate with us. Only in the place where God is with us can the purpose be fulfilled. Therefore, our responsibility cannot be fulfilled without God's cooperation. Ultimately, the completion of our responsibility is also through God's cooperation, and the initiation of our responsibility is also through God's cooperation; from that process to the result, it must also go through God's cooperation.

We humans often say, "I am lucky." You all often use such words. "Today, I was lucky." We say such things. Where does that luck come from? Did you move to make yourself lucky and meet that good day? Or did it turn out well even though you didn’t move like that? If we look at it this way, we do not say that we are lucky because we worked hard to achieve such results.

When we do something ordinary, but the results exceed that, we say, "I am lucky." This means that if one is born with a strong foundation of God's cooperation or the goodwill of ancestors, the person's life will inevitably show good results. In other words, if the content that can be good is contained in the motivation, it will appear as good results. Therefore, there will be many days in our lives where we feel lucky. When that happens, we see that person as a happy person. Just as individuals are like that, the same goes for nations.

Then, when we say that the Republic of Korea is lucky, or someone might say, "Oh, President Park is lucky." Then, will it end with that bad luck? Or will it end with something good? If the cause is good, the result should also be good, but if the result is bad, then this is definitely someone’s responsibility. This is not a matter of luck; it is a matter of human responsibility. If a person makes a mistake, no matter how good their fortune is, it can turn out badly. We can understand this.

From this perspective, the fall of humanity is also the same. When viewed from God's side, the most good being, the subject of the highest motivation, has led humanity to unhappiness through the process of results. Did humanity become unhappy because God did not cooperate? No, that is not the case. Did they become unhappy because the motivation was bad? That is also not the case. In other words, if humans make mistakes, the results can turn out badly.

In other words, if we examine carefully, if the motivation was good, it will definitely show good results through human life, but if we act hastily and focus on personal thoughts centered around our own desires, we can take a wrong path. They mention that the way to do this is to find a method, and they question what actions can be taken. The speaker emphasizes that it is not enough to only like those who belong to the Unification Church or only like Moon; everyone should be liked, including those from established churches. They explain that even if an enemy comes to a feast, the host must treat them as a guest to make the day sacred. The speaker insists that no matter how much they may dislike someone, they must treat them with respect when they appear as a guest.

The speaker continues to discuss the importance of enduring difficulties and mentions that if one can tolerate hardships, the history of misfortune will flow away. They stress that one cannot only like the members of the Unification Church or Moon; they must also make an effort to like members of established churches. The speaker warns that those who dislike this idea will face ruin, citing examples of people who opposed them and suffered consequences.

The speaker reflects on the nature of love and relationships, suggesting that true love extends beyond personal preferences. They argue that if one can love their family, they should also be able to love others, including those who may seem distant or different. The speaker believes that the Unification Church's philosophy is about creating a world where everyone is treated as family, transcending boundaries and divisions.

The speaker also emphasizes the importance of experiencing God's presence and understanding that true love is not limited to personal relationships but extends to all humanity. They argue that the Unification Church aims to create a world where everyone is seen as siblings, and this requires a shift in mindset.

The text goes on to discuss the historical context of struggles faced by humanity and the church, emphasizing that the Unification Church is not meant to be a solitary entity but rather a movement that seeks to unite all people under God's love. The speaker expresses a desire for a world where everyone can be friends and family, highlighting the importance of love and connection in achieving peace.

If I have a will, it will be, "I am the man who struggled until the very end, until the last moment of life, to avoid being indebted." This will be my epitaph. This will be my will. Do you understand?

If you want to repay debts, repay them, or if you do not want to, do not. If you want to repay, repay before all people. Then a new cultural world will be created from there, and a new heaven and earth will open the kingdom of peace.
We must take an offensive to avoid debt at the final front line.
Today, I appreciate your efforts in coming such a long way. Although I met busy passersby, the encounter we had today is not a coincidence. I referred to this meeting as the final front line, and this does not refer to the strategic front line of the Communist Party in this world, nor does it refer to the strategic Korean 38th parallel of the democratic world. We are aiming to take an offensive in front of the fundamental front line. What kind of offensive? An offensive to impose debts in order not to incur debts. If we proceed this way, we will achieve victory everywhere we go. As we go further, the fiercer the war becomes, the more the soldiers following me will increase day by day. This is a fact, and we cannot deny that behind Moon Am's persecution in America, there are increasingly more young followers. That is the principle of heaven. Do you understand? The Unification Church is developing despite opposition. That is an undeniable fact.

Now we understand what the final attack towards the final front line must be. Did you understand? "Yes." Do not incur debts with your eyes. Do not incur debts with your mouth, do not incur debts with your hands, do not incur debts with your heart, and do not incur debts with your face. Do not incur debts. While being self-disciplined, if there is any way to impose debts on my environment, I must know that it is my duty to act beyond time, beyond face and prestige, day and night, 24 hours. If we do this, our descendants will become those who can cover the world, and behind them will not arise a garden of lonely death, but a garden of flourishing peace. This is how it is viewed. Heaven begins from there... What is it? Where does heaven begin? "From the place of not incurring debts." From the place of not incurring debts, from the place of imposing debts...

Members of the Unification Church, you have incurred debts before the teacher, right? "Yes." You know the way to repay those debts, right? "Yes." Now, from now on in your village...

In 1976, when I go to America, I will engage in a fierce struggle. I will focus on the Yankee Stadium event on June 1st. That is the historic final front line. The final front line. Centered around America, which represents the democratic world, I will take the final offensive. Thus, by the time of the Washington event, if I can return in glory as a general in October, then my struggle will come to a conclusion. Do you understand? "Yes." Even if I have to walk with my feet worn out, clenching my teeth, I cannot stop my steps in the process of my suffering and my responsibility towards the world. Therefore, I can travel the world with a cane like others, and I can build a house and sing of the peaceful kingdom in such an era. Even if I live like that, I will die as a man who does not feel the pangs of conscience. This is how it is viewed. On that day, the Unification Church will develop even if I die, even if I do not work.

I hope you will be those who, through this strategy of offense, will commit all your strength to the final front line. You must say "Amen." Let's do it together. A- "Amen." Now, let those who say, "I will do that," raise their hands.

<Prayer> No matter how much struggling heroes and great figures there are, I have realized that the flowing time cannot be blocked. I have come to understand that it ends in failure when one emphasizes their own assertions. When I try to touch God's heart, I have now realized that what can block this is the group that struggles not to incur debts. When asked what the defense line of the final front line is, I have come to know that it is the soldiers fighting not to incur debts. When I go to the countryside, if there are people who impose debts on the farmers in the countryside, impose debts in all the environments they are in, impose debts on schoolmates and school authorities when they go to school, and if there are people who can impose debts in front of all the citizens of Gyeongbuk without incurring debts themselves, I have already understood that such people will surely enter the kingdom of heaven and have the qualification to become God's children. I have realized that without this offensive, we cannot make this world a world of peace.

I have come to understand that even Jesus, while dying on the cross, prayed, "Forgive them their sins," which was Jesus's final declaration to avoid incurring debts. Although he was born as the son of a carpenter and lived with fishermen on the shores of Galilee during his youth, he was tragically accused of being a traitor to his nation and died, but no one knew that the dead Jesus would manage the world and establish a cultural world.

Because he lived in a position that could align with the truth that could work with heavenly fortune, we have come to know that the power of that truth, the power of heavenly principles, established such a position.

Now, if I wish to prosper, I have resolved not to be someone who incurs debts. I have understood that the secret to prosperity is to impose debts, and I have now sworn to do so. I have made that resolution.

If the Daegu Church becomes a church that incurs debts before the national churches or the headquarters, we must understand that the hope for Daegu will be cut off. If all the branch churches in Gyeongbuk wish to incur debts to the Daegu headquarters church, let them understand that the fate of that church will ultimately be in jeopardy.

When we stand in a position where we can care for each other to avoid incurring debts, this will remain as a base of heaven, regardless of the church, the environment, the village, the family, the nation, or the world. We have now understood this, and we have resolved to do so. Heavenly Father, if there is a heart that seeks to benefit oneself and incur debts, please remove it even if it means striking it down. I earnestly hope that we will be equipped with the original posture to care for others and avoid incurring debts.

Now, when I return to my hometown, I earnestly hope that I will be a group that can practice from tomorrow with the overwhelming feelings and the resolution I have made. I hope to meet again on that day with victorious results to offer praise before heaven, and until then, I hope to be a group that continues to fight and advance while defending the front line, wishing for your protection and blessings to be even more abundant.

I earnestly ask that the grace and love of the eternal be with them forever, and I pray all these words in the name of True Parents. Amen.

<Words> Now, will you treat the guests to dinner, or not? Will you treat them to dinner, or not? "We will." Will you give them dinner, or not? "We will." Am I incurring a debt? I will not eat dinner to avoid incurring a debt. "We have incurred many debts." So, will you repay a little? "Yes." After doing that, will you say you didn't incur a debt? (Laughter) "No." Isn't that so? Then I will eat.

Shall we sing a song? "Yes." (Applause) We do it together, together. (Laughter) My throat hurts now, and if I sing, my head will hurt more. If I speak passionately, my head will hurt. So let's do it together. Shall we sing a vigorous song? "Yes." You know the song of the fighting man, right? (Singing "Wilderness Man") *
